Choose Section

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W14X159} \; &A &= 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 18.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 1580000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 311000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 162.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 102.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

Check Slenderness

\begin{aligned} \mathrm{col}_{section} &= \mathrm{W14X159} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam}_{section} &= \mathrm{W14X90} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{1} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 4000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 4000 \cdot mm } &= 197750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{2} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 3000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 3000 \cdot mm } &= 263666.667\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Ix}_{beam} }{ 7000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 416000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 7000 \cdot mm } &= 59428.571\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] G_{d} &= \frac{ \mathrm{column}_{1} + \mathrm{column}_{2} }{ \mathrm{beam} } = \frac{ 197750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} + 263666.667\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} }{ 59428.571\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 7.764 \\[10pt] G_{a} &= 1.000 \; \;\textrm{(Fixed)} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} k &= 1.800 \; \;\textrm{(From Alignment Chart)} \\[10pt] x &= \left( \frac{ \left( G_{d} \cdot G_{a} \cdot \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( G_{d} + G_{a} \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ \pi }{ k } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) } \right) \right) = \left( \frac{ \left( 7.764 \cdot 1.000 \cdot \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( 7.764 + 1.000 \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } \right) } \right) \right) &= 0.073 \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{SR} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ k \cdot l }{ r_{x} } ,\ k \cdot l \cdot \frac{1} { r_{y} } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 1.800 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} }{ 162.000\ \mathrm{mm} } ,\ 1.800 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \cdot \frac{1} { 102.000\ \mathrm{mm} } \right) } &= 70.588 \\[10pt] C_{c} &= \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot \mathrm{MPa} }{ f_{y} } } = \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot MPa }{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } } &= 126.169 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{SR} \lt C_{c} \rightarrow \left( 70.588 \lt 126.169 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Short} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 70.588 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 70.588 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.855 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 70.588 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.855 } \right) &= 123.259\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 70.588 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 206.690\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 206.690\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.924 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.924 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.924 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 17.454\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 123.259\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.924 \cdot \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.552 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.552 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.563 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.563 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 68.627 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 68.627 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.851 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 68.627 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.851 } \right) &= 124.104\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 68.627 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 218.669\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 218.669\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.920 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.920 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.920 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 17.454\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 124.104\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.920 \cdot \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.549 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.549 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.563 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.563 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W14X159} \; &A &= 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 18.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 1580000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 311000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 162.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 102.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

Check Slenderness

\begin{aligned} \mathrm{col}_{section} &= \mathrm{W14X159} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam}_{section} &= \mathrm{W18X86} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{1} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 4000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 4000 \cdot mm } &= 197750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{2} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 3000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 791000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 3000 \cdot mm } &= 263666.667\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Ix}_{beam} }{ 7000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 637000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 7000 \cdot mm } &= 91000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] G_{d} &= \frac{ \mathrm{column}_{1} + \mathrm{column}_{2} }{ \mathrm{beam} } = \frac{ 197750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} + 263666.667\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} }{ 91000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 5.071 \\[10pt] G_{a} &= 1.000 \; \;\textrm{(Fixed)} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} k &= 1.700 \; \;\textrm{(From Alignment Chart)} \\[10pt] x &= \left( \frac{ \left( G_{d} \cdot G_{a} \cdot \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( G_{d} + G_{a} \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ \pi }{ k } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) } \right) \right) = \left( \frac{ \left( 5.071 \cdot 1.000 \cdot \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.700 } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( 5.071 + 1.000 \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.700 } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.700 } \right) } \right) \right) &= 0.013 \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{SR} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ k \cdot l }{ r_{x} } ,\ k \cdot l \cdot \frac{1} { r_{y} } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 1.700 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} }{ 162.000\ \mathrm{mm} } ,\ 1.700 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \cdot \frac{1} { 102.000\ \mathrm{mm} } \right) } &= 66.667 \\[10pt] C_{c} &= \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot \mathrm{MPa} }{ f_{y} } } = \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot MPa }{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } } &= 126.169 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{SR} \lt C_{c} \rightarrow \left( 66.667 \lt 126.169 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Short} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 66.667 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.846 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.846 } \right) &= 124.942\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 231.721\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 231.721\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.915 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.915 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.915 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 17.454\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 124.942\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.915 \cdot \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.546 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.546 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.563 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.563 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 66.667 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.846 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.846 } \right) &= 124.942\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 30100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 66.667 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 231.721\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 231.721\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.915 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.915 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.915 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4160000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 381.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 396.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 17.454\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 5.029\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 124.942\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.915 \cdot \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.546 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.546 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 16.578\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 73.904\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.563 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.563 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Choose Section

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W18X130} \; &A &= 24700.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 490.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 30.500\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 17.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4200000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 818000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1020000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 116000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 204.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 68.600\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.909 } \right) &= 106.161\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 24700.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 20.202\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 107.872 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 88.505\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 20.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 88.505\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 1 \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4200000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 73.200\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 490.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.500\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 3.607\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 490.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 30.500\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 9.830\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{u} \gt l_{b} \gt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 9.830\ \mathrm{m} \gt 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \gt 3.607\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 2 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.60 \cdot f_{y} = 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 20.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 106.161\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 1 \cdot \left( \frac{ 73.200\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.682 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.682 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 20.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 73.200\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.628 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.628 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W18X130} \; &A &= 24700.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 490.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 284.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 30.500\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 17.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4200000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 818000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1020000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 116000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 204.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 68.600\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.907 } \right) &= 107.284\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 19800.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 105.548 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 92.445\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 92.445\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 1 \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4230000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 4.128\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.640\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 4.128\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 107.284\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 1 \cdot \left( \frac{ 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.679 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.679 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.613 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.613 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Choose Section

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W24X104} \; &A &= 19800.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 12.700\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4230000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 667000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1290000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 108000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 257.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 73.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W24X104} \; &A &= 19800.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 12.700\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4230000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 667000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1290000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 108000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 257.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 73.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

\;\textrm{(Fixed)} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} k &= 1.900 \; \;\textrm{(From Alignment Chart)} \\[10pt] x &= \left( \frac{ \left( G_{d} \cdot G_{a} \cdot \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( G_{d} + G_{a} \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ \pi }{ k } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) } \right) \right) = \left( \frac{ \left( 11.837 \cdot 1.000 \cdot \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.900 } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( 11.837 + 1.000 \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.900 } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.900 } \right) } \right) \right) &= 0.090 \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{SR} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ k \cdot l }{ r_{x} } ,\ k \cdot l \cdot \frac{1} { r_{y} } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 1.900 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} }{ 257.000\ \mathrm{mm} } ,\ 1.900 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \cdot \frac{1} { 73.900\ \mathrm{mm} } \right) } &= 102.842 \\[10pt] C_{c} &= \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot \mathrm{MPa} }{ f_{y} } } = \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot MPa }{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } } &= 126.169 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{SR} \lt C_{c} \rightarrow \left( 102.842 \lt 126.169 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Short} \; 19800.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 100.135 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 102.709\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 102.709\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 1 \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4230000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 4.128\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 612.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 325.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 19.100\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.640\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 4.128\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 109.868\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 1 \cdot \left( \frac{ 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.673 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.673 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 25.202\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 72.681\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.613 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.613 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W12X190} \; &A &= 36100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 366.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 44.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 26.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4310000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 1520000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 787000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 245000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 148.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 82.600\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W12X190} \; &A &= 36100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 366.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 44.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 26.900\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4310000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 1520000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 787000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 245000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 148.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 82.600\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

Check Slenderness

\begin{aligned} \mathrm{col}_{section} &= \mathrm{W12X190} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam}_{section} &= \mathrm{W12X120} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{1} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 4000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 787000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 4000 \cdot mm } &= 196750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{2} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 3000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 787000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 3000 \cdot mm } &= 262333.333\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Ix}_{beam} }{ 7000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 445000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 7000 \cdot mm } &= 63571.429\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] G_{d} &= \frac{ \mathrm{column}_{1} + \mathrm{column}_{2} }{ \mathrm{beam} } = \frac{ 196750.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} + 262333.333\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} }{ 63571.429\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 7.222 \\[10pt] G_{a} &= 1.000 \; \;\textrm{(Fixed)} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} k &= 1.800 \; \;\textrm{(From Alignment Chart)} \\[10pt] x &= \left( \frac{ \left( G_{d} \cdot G_{a} \cdot \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( G_{d} + G_{a} \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ \pi }{ k } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) } \right) \right) = \left( \frac{ \left( 7.222 \cdot 1.000 \cdot \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( 7.222 + 1.000 \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.800 } \right) } \right) \right) &= 0.024 \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{SR} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ k \cdot l }{ r_{x} } ,\ k \cdot l \cdot \frac{1} { r_{y} } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 1.800 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} }{ 148.000\ \mathrm{mm} } ,\ 1.800 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \cdot \frac{1} { 82.600\ \mathrm{mm} } \right) } &= 87.167 \\[10pt] C_{c} &= \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot \mathrm{MPa} }{ f_{y} } } = \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot MPa }{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } } &= 126.169 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{SR} \lt C_{c} \rightarrow \left( 87.167 \lt 126.169 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Short} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 87.167 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 87.167 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.885 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 87.167 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.885 } \right) &= 115.895\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 36100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 87.167 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 135.543\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 135.543\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.947 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.947 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.947 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 115.895\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.947 \cdot \left( \frac{ 71.332\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.532 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.532 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 71.332\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.529 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.529 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 84.746 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 84.746 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.881 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 84.746 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.881 } \right) &= 116.995\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 36100.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 84.746 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 143.399\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 143.399\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.941 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.941 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.941 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4310000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 71.332\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 366.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 44.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 4.102\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 366.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 323.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 44.200\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 21.690\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 4.102\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 116.995\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.941 \cdot \left( \frac{ 71.332\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.528 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.528 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 13.823\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 71.332\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.529 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.529 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

23200.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 102.426 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 98.167\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 98.167\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 1 \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4470000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 4.001\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 7.756\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 4.001\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 108.779\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 1 \cdot \left( \frac{ 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.618 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.618 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.565 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.565 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Choose Section

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W21X122} \; &A &= 23200.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 15.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4470000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 806000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1230000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 127000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 231.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 74.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

\\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } &= 1.667 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ F_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - 0 \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.667 } \right) &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] F_{a_{}} &= 0.8 \cdot F_{a} = 0.8 \cdot 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= F_{a_{}} \cdot 0.5 = 119.040\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Area}_{req} &= \frac{ p }{ f_{a} } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 59.520\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 8383.737\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \\[10pt] F_{b} &= 0.6 \cdot F_{y} = 0.6 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{b} &= F_{b} \cdot 0.5 = 148.800\ \mathrm{MPa} \cdot 0.5 &= 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Sx}_{req} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ f_{b} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 74.400\ \mathrm{MPa} } &= 4132258.065\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{name} &= \mathrm{W21X122} \; &A &= 23200.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} \; &d &= 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] b_{f} &= 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{f} &= 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} \; &t_{w} &= 15.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] S_{x} &= 4470000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &S_{y} &= 806000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \; &I_{x} &= 1230000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; \\[10pt] I_{y} &= 127000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} \; &r_{x} &= 231.000\ \mathrm{mm} \; &r_{y} &= 74.200\ \mathrm{mm} \; \\[10pt] m_{u} &= 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} \; &f_{y} &= 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} \; &\mathrm{axial} &= 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} \; \\[10pt] \end{aligned}

Check Slenderness

\begin{aligned} \mathrm{col}_{section} &= \mathrm{W21X122} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam}_{section} &= \mathrm{W14X109} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{1} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 4000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 1230000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 4000 \cdot mm } &= 307500.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{column}_{2} &= \frac{ I_{x} }{ 3000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 1230000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 3000 \cdot mm } &= 410000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] \mathrm{beam} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Ix}_{beam} }{ 7000 \cdot \mathrm{mm} } = \frac{ 516000000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{4} }{ 7000 \cdot mm } &= 73714.286\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} \\[10pt] G_{d} &= \frac{ \mathrm{column}_{1} + \mathrm{column}_{2} }{ \mathrm{beam} } = \frac{ 307500.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} + 410000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} }{ 73714.286\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 9.734 \\[10pt] G_{a} &= 1.000 \; \;\textrm{(Fixed)} \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} k &= 1.850 \; \;\textrm{(From Alignment Chart)} \\[10pt] x &= \left( \frac{ \left( G_{d} \cdot G_{a} \cdot \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( G_{d} + G_{a} \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ \pi }{ k } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ \pi }{ k } \right) } \right) \right) = \left( \frac{ \left( 9.734 \cdot 1.000 \cdot \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.850 } \right) ^{ 2 } \right) - 36 }{ 6 \cdot \left( 9.734 + 1.000 \right) } - \left( \frac{ \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.850 } }{ \tan \left( \frac{ 3.142 }{ 1.850 } \right) } \right) \right) &= 0.094 \end{aligned} \begin{aligned} \mathrm{SR} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ k \cdot l }{ r_{x} } ,\ k \cdot l \cdot \frac{1} { r_{y} } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 1.850 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} }{ 231.000\ \mathrm{mm} } ,\ 1.850 \cdot 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \cdot \frac{1} { 74.200\ \mathrm{mm} } \right) } &= 99.730 \\[10pt] C_{c} &= \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot \mathrm{MPa} }{ f_{y} } } = \sqrt { \frac{ 2 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200000 \cdot MPa }{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } } &= 126.169 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{SR} \lt C_{c} \rightarrow \left( 99.730 \lt 126.169 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Short} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 99.730 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 99.730 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.901 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 99.730 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.901 } \right) &= 110.060\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 23200.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 99.730 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 103.545\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 103.545\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 1 \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4470000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 4.001\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 551.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 315.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 24.400\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 7.756\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 4.001\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 110.060\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 1 \cdot \left( \frac{ 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.616 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.616 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 21.509\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 68.779\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.565 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.565 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}

Stability and Strength Check

\begin{aligned} F_{s} &= \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ \mathrm{SR} }{ 8 \cdot C_{c} } \right) - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( C_{c} \right) ^{ 3 } } = \frac{ 5 }{ 3 } + \left( 3 \cdot \frac{ 72.549 }{ 8 \cdot 126.169 } \right) - \frac{ \left( 72.549 \right) ^{ 3 } }{ 8 \cdot \left( 126.169 \right) ^{ 3 } } &= 1.859 \\[10pt] F_{a} &= \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot C_{c} \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{y} }{ F_{s} } \right) = \left( 1 - \frac{ \left( 72.549 \right) ^{ 2 } }{ \left( 2 \cdot 126.169 \right) ^{ 2 } } \right) \cdot \left( \frac{ 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 1.859 } \right) &= 122.409\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] f_{a} &= \frac{ \mathrm{axial} }{ A } = \frac{ 499.000\ \mathrm{kN} }{ 33400.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{2} } &= 14.940\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Fe}_{x} &= \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( \pi \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot E_{s} }{ 23 \cdot \left( \mathrm{SR} \right) ^{ 2 } } = \frac{ 12 \cdot \left( 3.142 \right) ^{ 2 } \cdot 200.000\ \mathrm{GPa} }{ 23 \cdot \left( 72.549 \right) ^{ 2 } } &= 195.668\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= \frac{ \mathrm{Cm} }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ \mathrm{Fe}_{x} } \right) } = \frac{ 0.850 }{ 1 - \left( \frac{ 14.940\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 195.668\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) } &= 0.920 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.920 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} &= 0.920 \; \\[10pt] f_{bx} &= \frac{ m_{x} }{ S_{x} } = \frac{ 307.440\ \mathrm{kN} \cdot \mathrm{m} }{ 4600000.000\ \mathrm{mm}^{3} } &= 66.835\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] l_{c} &= \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{min} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 399.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 386.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 399.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 33.300\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 5.067\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] l_{u} &= \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot b_{f} }{ \sqrt { \mathrm{fy} } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ \mathrm{fy} \cdot d }{ b_{f} \cdot t_{f} } } \right) } = \operatorname{max} { \left( \frac{ 200 \cdot 399.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ \sqrt { 248 } } ,\ 137900 \cdot \frac{1} { \frac{ 248 \cdot 386.000\ \mathrm{mm} }{ 399.000\ \mathrm{mm} \cdot 33.300\ \mathrm{mm} } } \right) } &= 19.140\ \mathrm{m} \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } l_{b} \lt l_{c} \rightarrow \left( 4.000\ \mathrm{m} \lt 5.067\ \mathrm{m} \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{case} &= 1 \; \\[10pt] F_{bx} &= 0.66 \cdot f_{y} = 0.66 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} &= 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} \\[10pt] \mathrm{Stability} &= \frac{ f_{a} }{ F_{a} } + \mathrm{Magnification}_{factor} \cdot \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \frac{ 14.940\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 122.409\ \mathrm{MPa} } + 0.920 \cdot \left( \frac{ 66.835\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.498 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Stability} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.498 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \\[10pt] \mathrm{Strenght} &= \left( \frac{ f_{a} }{ 0.60 \cdot f_{y} } \right) + \left( \frac{ f_{bx} }{ F_{bx} } \right) = \left( \frac{ 14.940\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 0.60 \cdot 248.000\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) + \left( \frac{ 66.835\ \mathrm{MPa} }{ 163.680\ \mathrm{MPa} } \right) &= 0.509 \\[10pt] &\text{Since, } \mathrm{Strenght} \lt 1 \rightarrow \left( 0.509 \lt 1 \right) : \\[10pt] \mathrm{Column} &= \mathrm{Safe} \; \end{aligned}
